package "io.vertigo.studio.domain.security"



create Task TkLoadBaseIndex {
	className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect",
	request : """	select 	bas.BASE_ID, 
						bas.NAME, 
						bas.CODE, 
						bas.CREATION_DATE, 
						bas.TAGS,
						bas.GEO_LOCATION,  
						bastype.LABEL as BASE_TYPE_LABEL
				from BASE bas
				join BASE_TYPE bastype on bastype.base_type_id = bas.base_type_id
				where BASE_ID in (#baseIds.rownum#);"""
	in 	baseIds 	{domain : DoId, 		cardinality: "*"} 
	out	dtcIndex	{domain : DoDtBaseIndex cardinality: "*"} 
}

create DtDefinition DtRecord {
	stereotype : "KeyConcept"
	id	  dosId			{domain: DoId 		label: "Id"}
	
	field regId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Region" 		cardinality:"?" }
  	field depId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Departement" 	cardinality:"?" }
  	field comId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Commune" 		cardinality:"?" }
  
  	field typId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Record type" 	cardinality:"1"}
	field title 		{domain: DoString 	label: "Title" 			cardinality:"1"}
	field amount 		{domain: DoConso 	label: "Amount" 		cardinality:"1"}
	field utiIdOwner 	{domain: DoId 		label: "Owner" 			cardinality:"1" }
  
  	field etaCd 		{domain: DoString 	label: "State" 			cardinality:"1"}	
}

create Domain DoId {
	dataType : Long
	storeType : "NUMERIC"
}

create Domain DoMultipleIds {
	dataType : String
    storeType : "TEXT"
}



create Domain DoInstant {
	dataType : Instant
	storeType : "TIMESTAMP"
}

create Domain DoLocaldate {
	dataType : LocalDate
	storeType : "DATE"
}


create Domain DoCurrency {
	dataType : BigDecimal
	unit : "$"
	storeType: "NUMERIC(12,2)"
}


create Domain DoHealth {
	dataType: Integer
	storeType : "NUMERIC"
}

create Domain DoLabel {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "VARCHAR(100)"
	indexType : "text_fr:sortable"
}

create Domain DoDescription {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "VARCHAR(350)"
	indexType : "text_fr"
}

create Domain DoEmail {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "VARCHAR(150)"
}

create Domain DoUrl {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "TEXT"
}

create Domain DoCode {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "VARCHAR(100)"
	indexType : "code:keyword"
}


create Domain DoPassword {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "VARCHAR(32)"
}

create Domain DoText {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "TEXT"
}

create Domain DoFilePath {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "VARCHAR(500)"
}

create Domain DoFileData {
	dataType : DataStream
	storeType : "bytea"
}

create Domain DoTags {
	dataType : String
	storeType : "TEXT"
	indexType : "multiple_code:facetable"
}

create Domain DoYesNo {
	dataType : Boolean
	storeType : "bool"
}


create Domain DoSize {
	dataType : Long
	storeType : "NUMERIC"
}

	dataType : Long
	storeType : "NUMERIC"
}

	dataType : ValueObject
	type : "io.mars.support.smarttypes.GeoPoint"
	storeType : "TEXT"
}

create Task TkSelectEquipmentType {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
            select EQUIPMENT_TYPE_ID, LABEL, EQUIPMENT_CATEGORY_ID from EQUIPMENT_TYPE
             """
    out dtcEquipmentType     {domain : DoDtEquipmentType cardinality: "*" }
}

create Task TkGetBaseManager {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
            select per.*
            	from mission mis
            	join person per on mis.person_id = per.person_id
            	where mis.base_id = #baseId# and mis.role_id= 'MANAG'
            	limit 1;
             """
    in 	baseId   {domain : DoId         cardinality: "1"}
    out manager  {domain : DoDtPerson 	cardinality: "?"}
}


create Task TkGetMissionsDisplayByPersonId {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
           select 
            		mis.mission_id as MISSION_ID,
            		rol.label as ROLE,
            		bas.name as BASE_NAME,
            		bus.name as BUSINESS_NAME
            	from mission mis
                left join role rol on mis.role_id = rol.role_id
            	left join base bas on mis.base_id = bas.base_id
				left join business bus on mis.business_id = bus.business_id
            	where mis.person_id = #personId#;
             """
    in	personId     {domain : DoId         		cardinality: "1" }
    out missions     {domain : DoDtMissionDisplay   cardinality: "*" }
}
create Task TkGetLastTicketsByBaseId {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
            select 
            	tic.*
			from ticket tic
			join equipment equ on equ.equipment_id = tic.equipment_id
			where equ.base_id = #baseId#
			order by tic.date_created desc
			limit 50
             """
    in 	baseId 	{domain : DoId         	cardinality: "1" }
    out tickets {domain : DoDtTicket    cardinality: "*" }
}

create Task TkGetLastTickets {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
            select 
            	tic.*
			from ticket tic
			order by tic.date_created desc
			limit 50
             """
    out  tickets     {domain : DoDtTicket    cardinality: "*"}
}

create Task TkGetLastWorkOrders {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
            select 
            	wor.*
			from work_order wor
			order by wor.date_created desc
			limit 20
             """
    out workOrders     {domain : DoDtWorkOrder    cardinality: "*"}
}

create DtDefinition DtOpendataSet {
	id odsId 			{domain: DoId 			label:"Id"}
	field code 			{domain: DoCode 		label: "Code" 					}
	field title 		{domain: DoLabel 		label: "Title" 					}
	field description 	{domain: DoDescription 	label: "Description" 			}
	field endPointUrl 	{domain: DoUrl 			label:"Service Endpoint URL" 	}
	field picturefileId {domain: DoId 			label:"Picture" 				}
	field tags 			{domain: DoMultipleIds 	label: "Tags" 					}
}

	stereotype: "StaticMasterData"
	id opendataSetStatusId 		{domain: DoCode 		label:"Id"}
	field label				 	{domain: DoLabel 		label:"Status Label" 	}
}

create Association AOpendataSetOpendataSetStatus {
	fkFieldName : "opendataSetStatusId"
    
 	dtDefinitionA : DtOpendataSet
 	type : "*>?"
	dtDefinitionB : DtOpendataSetStatus
			
	labelB : "Opendata Set Status"
}

create DtDefinition DtTicket {
	id ticketId {domain: DoId label:"Id"}
	field code {domain: DoLabel label: "Number" }
	field title {domain: DoLabel label: "Title" }
	field description {domain: DoDescription label: "Description" }
	field dateCreated {domain: DoLocaldate label: "Creation Date" }
	field dateClosed {domain: DoLocaldate label: "Closing Date" }
}

create DtDefinition DtWorkOrder {
	id woId {domain: DoId label:"Id"}
	field code {domain: DoLabel label: "Code" }
	field ticketCode {domain: DoLabel label: "Number" }
	field name {domain: DoLabel label: "Name" }
	field description {domain: DoDescription label: "Description" }
	field dateCreated {domain: DoLocaldate label: "Creation Date" }
	field dateClosed {domain: DoLocaldate label: "Closing Date" }
	field dueDate {domain: DoLocaldate label: "Due Date" }	
}

}

	field label {domain: DoLabel label:"Status Label" }
}

	range r2 { filter:"geoLocation:#geoLocation#~10km", label:"< 10km"},
	range r3 { filter:"geoLocation:#geoLocation#~20km", label:"< 20km"},
	range r4 { filter:"geoLocation:#geoLocation#~50km", label:"< 50km"},
	range r5 { filter:"geoLocation:#geoLocation#~100km", label:"< 100km"},
	range r6 { filter:"geoLocation:#geoLocation#~200km", label:"< 200km"},
	range r7 { filter:"geoLocation:#geoLocation#~500km", label:"< 500km"},
	range r8 { filter:"geoLocation:[#geoLocation#~500km to #geoLocation#~0km]", label:"> 500km"}	
}

create Task TkGetEquipmentsOverview {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
            select 
            	count(1) as count,
            	bus.business_id as business_id,
            	bus.name as business_name,
            	bus.icon as business_icon,
            	sum(case when equ.health_level >= 30 then 1 else 0 end) as ok_count,
            	sum(case when equ.health_level < 30 then 1 else 0 end) as down_count
			from equipment equ
				join business bus on bus.business_id = equ.business_id 
			where equ.base_id = #baseId#
			group by business_name, bus.business_id
             """
    in 	baseId     {domain : DoId         			cardinality: "1"  }
    out overview   {domain : DoDtEquipmentOverview  cardinality: "*"  }
}

create Task TkGetBasesSummary {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
            select 
				(select count(*) from base) as base_count,
				(select avg(health_level) from base) as base_mean_health,
				(select count(*) from ticket tic where tic.ticket_status_id = 'OPEN' or tic.ticket_status_id = 'ASSIGNED') as opened_tickets,
				(select sum(case when health_level > 30 then 1.0 else 0.0 end) / count(*) * 100 from equipment) as online_equipment_percent;
             """
    out basesSummary     {domain : DoDtBasesSummary    cardinality: "1" }
}

create Task TkGetBaseOverview {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
           select 
				(select count(*) from equipment equ where equ.base_id = #baseId#) as equipment_count,
				(select count(*) from ticket tic join equipment equ on equ.equipment_id = tic.equipment_id where equ.base_id = #baseId# and ( tic.ticket_status_id = 'OPEN' or tic.ticket_status_id = 'ASSIGNED')) as opened_tickets,
				(select count(*) from work_order wor join ticket tic on tic.ticket_id = wor.ticket_id join equipment equ on equ.equipment_id = tic.equipment_id where equ.base_id = #baseId#  and wor.work_order_status_id = 'INPROGRESS') as work_orders_inprogress
             """
    in 	baseId     		{domain : DoId    				cardinality: "1"  }
    out baseOverview    {domain : DoDtBaseOverview    	cardinality: "1"  }
}


create Task TkGetEquipmentMaintenanceOverview {  
    className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect"
    request : """
           select 
				(select count(*) from ticket tic where tic.equipment_id = #equipmentId# and ( tic.ticket_status_id = 'OPEN' or tic.ticket_status_id = 'ASSIGNED')) as opened_tickets,
				(select count(*) from work_order wor join ticket tic on tic.ticket_id = wor.ticket_id join equipment equ on equ.equipment_id = #equipmentId#  and wor.work_order_status_id = 'INPROGRESS') as work_orders_inprogress
             """
    in 	equipmentId     				{domain : DoId    							cardinality: "1" }
    out equipmentMaintenanceOverview    {domain : DoDtEquipmentMaintenanceOverview  cardinality: "1" }
}

create Task TkLoadBaseIndex {
	className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect",
	request : """	select 	bas.BASE_ID, 
						bas.NaAME, 
						bas.CODE, 
						bas.CREATION_DATE, 
						bas.TAGS,
						bas.GEO_LOCATION,  
						bastype.LABEL as BASE_TYPE_LABEL
				from BASE bas
				join BASE_TYPE bastype on bastype.base_type_id = bas.base_type_id
				where BASE_ID in (#baseIds.rownum#);"""
	in 	baseIds 	{domain : DoId, 		cardinality: "*"} 
	out	dtcIndex	{domain : DoDtBaseIndex cardinality: "*"} 
}


create Task TkLoadEquipmentIndex {
	className : "io.vertigo.basics.task.TaskEngineSelect",
	request : """	select 	equ.EQUIPMENT_ID,
						equ.NAME, 
						equ.CODE, 
						equ.PURCHASE_DATE, 
						equ.TAGS, 
						equ.GEO_LOCATION,  
						equipmentType.LABEL as EQUIPMENT_TYPE_NAME,
						equipmentCategory.LABEL as EQUIPMENT_CATEGORY_NAME,
                        bas.NAME as BASE_NAME
				from EQUIPMENT equ
                join BASE bas on bas.base_id = equ.base_id
                join EQUIPMENT_TYPE equipmentType on equipmentType.equipment_type_id = equ.equipment_type_id
				join EQUIPMENT_CATEGORY equipmentCategory on equipmentCategory.equipment_category_id = equipmentType.equipment_category_id
				where EQUIPMENT_ID in (#equipmentIds.rownum#);"""
	in 	equipmentIds 	{domain : DoId, cardinality: "*"} 
	out dtcIndex 		{domain : DoDtEquipmentIndex, cardinality: "*"} 
}

# /*ghfdghdgfhdf */

#	values : `{		"enabled" : 	{ "opendataSetStatusId" : "ENABLED", 	"label" : "Enabled" },
#        			"disabled" : 	{ "opendataSetStatusId" : "DISABLED", 	"label" : "Disabled"}}`

#	values : ` { 	"done" : 		{ "workOrderStatusId" : "DONE", 		"label" : "Done" 		},
#        			"inProgress" : 	{ "workOrderStatusId" : "INPROGRESS",  	"label" : "In Progress" },
#        			"failed" : 		{ "workOrderStatusId" : "FAILED", 		"label" : "Failed"		},
#        			"pending" : 	{ "workOrderStatusId" : "PENDING", 		"label" : "Pending" 	}}`
